Wall 8:
Powerful Intel i9 CPU, 8 x 4K output, up to 32 x 1080p display support
Supports up to 4 x 4K HDMI input
Hot-swap redundant power supply for 24/7 reliability
Advanced automation protocols: KNX, DALI, RS232, DMX512
Designer V5 software for unlimited scenario design
Wall28:
User-friendly operation with robust Designer V5 software
Full HD input/output for versatile applications
Ideal for command centers, monitoring, and meeting rooms
